<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Exhibit 99.1</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="border-collapse:collapse; width:21.08%;">
<tr>
<td style="width:21.08%;"></td>
</tr>
<tr style="height:35.5pt;">
<td valign="top" >
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:0pt;;text-indent:0pt;;color:#595959;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><img src="g1ujw3hod4qr000001.jpg" title="" alt="" style="width:143px;height:47px;"></p></td>
</tr>
</table></div>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Annexon Biosciences Reports Fourth Quarter and Full-Year 2020 Financial Results </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">with Recent Business Highlights</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">SOUTH SAN FRANCISCO, Calif., March 25, 2021<font style="font-weight:normal;"> &#8211; Today Annexon, Inc.&nbsp;&nbsp;(&#8220;Annexon&#8221;) (Nasdaq: ANNX), a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company developing a pipeline of novel therapies for patients with classical complement-mediated disorders of the body, brain and eye, announced fourth quarter and full-year 2020 financial results and business highlights. </font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Recent Business Highlights</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Annexon continues to make strong progress in advancing its broad and deep pipeline and clinical programs across a&nbsp;&nbsp;range of potential indications.&nbsp;&nbsp;Recent highlights include: </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:9pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font><font style="font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">ANX005 in Guillain-Barr&#233; Syndrome (GBS).&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font style="color:#000000;">In March 2021, the company completed evaluation of its drug-drug interaction (DDI) study of ANX005 co-administered with Intravenous Immunoglobulin (IVIg) in 14 patients with GBS.&nbsp;&nbsp;The DDI study was conducted to evaluate the safety and tolerability of ANX005 and IVIg co-administration in GBS patients, and measured pharmacokinetics (PK) and pharmacodynamics (PD) of ANX005 when administered in combination with IVIg.&nbsp;&nbsp;IVIg, though not FDA-approved in the United States for GBS, is currently the standard of care for GBS.&nbsp;&nbsp;Initial results from the DDI study included: </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:10%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:Courier New;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:Courier New;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">o</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Co-administration of IVIg-ANX005 was well-tolerated.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:10%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:Courier New;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:Courier New;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">o</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Co-administration of IVIg-ANX005 achieved full C1q target engagement, and C1q suppression was maintained within the targeted range.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:10%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:Courier New;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:10pt;font-family:Courier New;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">o</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">The open-label DDI study was not placebo-controlled or powered for statistical significance on efficacy measures.&nbsp;&nbsp;A number of key GBS outcome measures were recorded from baseline, and early improvement was observed in GBS patients, including increased muscle strength, decreased neurofilament light chain (NfL) and improved GBS disability score.  </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:3.33%;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Full results from the DDI study are expected to be submitted to a peer-reviewed forum in 2021.&nbsp;&nbsp;A placebo-controlled Phase 2/3 trial is ongoing to evaluate the efficacy of ANX005 monotherapy in improving disability in GBS patients.&nbsp;&nbsp;Data from the Phase 2/3 trial is anticipated in 2023.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:6.67%;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:9pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font><font style="font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">ANX007 in Geographic Atrophy (GA). </font><font style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;color:#1C262C;"> </font><font style="color:#000000;">In February 2021, the company initiated a Phase 2 trial evaluating the efficacy of ANX007 in reducing the area of GA as evaluated by fundus autofluorescence (FAF) in patients with GA, which includes monthly and every other month dosing of ANX007.&nbsp;&nbsp;Data from this trial is anticipated in 2023.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>

<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;We continue to make progress against our vision of building a leading, multi-faceted complement therapeutics company with an innovative portfolio for a broad range of autoimmune, neurodegenerative and ophthalmic diseases,&#8221; said Douglas Love, Esq., president and chief executive officer of Annexon.&nbsp;&nbsp;&#8220;The DDI data gives us further confidence in ANX005.&nbsp;&nbsp;We are rapidly advancing multiple Phase 2 clinical programs across a diverse set of potential indications, and accelerating development of a number of innovative, next generation product candidates.&nbsp;&nbsp;This clinical momentum coupled with our strong capital position positions us well to drive value in 2021 and beyond.&#8221;</p>

Net loss was $63.4 million for the year ended December 31, 2020 compared to $37.2 million for the year ended December 31, 2019.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">About Annexon, Inc.</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:6pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Annexon is a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company developing a pipeline of novel therapies for patients with classical complement-mediated disorders of the body, brain and eye. The company&#8217;s pipeline is based on its platform technology addressing well-researched classical complement-mediated autoimmune and neurodegenerative disease processes, both of which are triggered by aberrant activation of C1q, the initiating molecule of the classical complement pathway. Annexon is deploying a disciplined, biomarker-driven strategy designed to select indications, identify patients and to measure target engagement and response to treatment with its drug candidates.  For more information, visit <font style="text-decoration:underline;">www.annexonbio.com</font>.</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Forward Looking Statements</p>
